          googletag.pubads().setTargeting('variant', window.ab_testing);
        }
        var tracking = [];
        var all_tests_on_page = document.querySelectorAll('[id^="ab_id_"]');
        for (var i = 0, len = all_tests_on_page.length; i < len; i++) {
          tracking.push(all_tests_on_page[i].dataset['optimizely']);
        }
        if (tracking.length >= 1){
          googletag.pubads().setTargeting('OPTMZVAR', tracking.join(","));
        }
        googletag.pubads().setCategoryExclusion('Lead Score 501-1000');
        googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
        googletag.enableServices();
        googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotOnload', handleSlotOnLoad);
        window.ads_library.initialized = true;
      });

    const handleSlotOnLoad = (event) => {
      const slot = event && event.slot;
      updateFluidAd(slot);
    };

    const updateFluidAd = (slot) => {
      const elementId = slot && slot.getSlotElementId && slot.getSlotElementId();
      const slotDiv = elementId && document.getElementById(elementId);
      const iframe = slotDiv && slotDiv.children && slotDiv.children[0] && slotDiv.children[0].children[0];
      const minWidth = iframe && iframe.style && iframe.style.minWidth;
      const isFluidAd = minWidth === '100%';

      const isPhotoMrect1 = elementId === 'div-gpt-ad-PHOTOMRECT1';
      if (isPhotoMrect1 && slotDiv) {
        if (isFluidAd) {
          slotDiv.classList.add('ads-photomrect1-fluid');
        } else {
          slotDiv.classList.remove('ads-photomrect1-fluid');
        }
      }
    };

    var preloadAds = function() {
      googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        window.gptAds.gptadslotsPreload.targets.forEach(function(slot) {
          googletag.display(slot.getSlotElementId());
        });
        googletag.pubads().refresh(window.gptAds.gptadslotsPreload.targets);
      });
    };

    var preloadTile1AdForView = function(adSlotForView) {
      if (!adSlotForView.isLoaded) {
        adSlotForView.targets.forEach(function(slot) {
            googletag.display(slot.getSlotElementId());
        });
        adSlotForView.isLoaded = true;
      }
      googletag.pubads().refresh(adSlotForView.targets);
      window.SRPPreloadTile1Ad = true;
    };

    var mapView = function() {
      var body = document.getElementsByTagName("BODY");
      if (body.length) {
        return body[0].classList.contains('ab-mixed-view');
      }
      return false;
    };

    var preloadTile1Ad = function(view) {
      googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        if (view === 'list') {
          if (!mapView())
            preloadTile1AdForView(window.gptAds.gptadslotsTILE1PreloadListView);
        }
        else {
          if (mapView())
            preloadTile1AdForView(window.gptAds.gptadslotsTILE1PreloadMapView);
        }
      });
    };

    var setFluidTileAd = function(adUnit) {
      try
      {
        let adDivId = 'div-gpt-ad-TILE';
        adDivId += mapView() ? 'MAP' : 'LIST';
        adDivId = adUnit.replace('TILE', adDivId);
        let tileAd = document.getElementById(adDivId);
        if (tileAd) {
          tileAd.parentElement.parentElement.classList.add("fluid_tile_ad");
        }
      }
      catch(e) { /* ignore */ }
    };

    var setTxtLdp1bAdWidth = function(width) {
      var widthPx = width + 'px';
      var txtldp1bAd = document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-TXTLDP1B');
      txtldp1bAd.style.width = widthPx;
      setTimeout(
        function() {
          txtldp1bAd.classList.remove("TXTLDPLoading");
          document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-TXTLDP1').classList.remove("TXTLDPLoading");
        }, 300
      );
    };

    var handlePreloadAdsMessage = function (event) {
      try
      {
        let origin = event.origin || event.originalEvent.origin;
        //tpc.googlesyndication.com is another CDN of gpt ads static files
        if (origin && origin.indexOf('.googlesyndication.com') !== -1) {
          let jsonMsg = JSON.parse(event.data);
          switch (jsonMsg.type) {
            case 'FLUIDTILE':
              setFluidTileAd(jsonMsg.ad_unit);
              break;
            case 'TXTLDP1B':
              setTxtLdp1bAdWidth(jsonMsg.width);
              break;
          }
        }
      }
      catch(e) { /* ignore */ }
    };

    defineAdSlots();
    window.addEventListener("message", handlePreloadAdsMessage, false);
  </script>

function tapadSrc(partnerId, deviceId) {
  return "https://pixel.tapad.com/idsync/ex/receive?partner_id=" +
    partnerId + "&partner_device_id=" + deviceId;
}

function checkAndSend(retries, partnerId, deviceIdGetter) {
  try {
    var deviceId = deviceIdGetter();

    if (!deviceId && retries > 0) {
      return setTimeout(function() {
        checkAndSend(retries - 1, partnerId, deviceIdGetter);
      }, 250);
    }

    (new Image()).src = tapadSrc(partnerId, deviceId);
  } catch (err) {
    _satellite.logger.error('Tapad error: ' + err.message);
  }
}

function getCookie(cname) {
   var name = cname + "=";
   var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
   for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
       var c = ca[i];
       while (c.charAt(0)==' ') {
           c = c.substring(1);
       }
       if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
           return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
       }
   }
   return "";
}
//Initializetheobject
    ncg_data=window.ncg_data||{};
function getLogin(loginData) {
    if (!loginData) return "";
   var name = "pID=";
   var ca = loginData.split('&');
   for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
       var c = ca[i];
       while (c.charAt(0)==' ') {
           c = c.substring(1);
       }
       if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
           return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
       }
   }
   return "";
}
